\hypertarget{interface_thing_smart_scene_manager}{}\doxysection{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Manager Class Reference}
\label{interface_thing_smart_scene_manager}\index{ThingSmartSceneManager@{ThingSmartSceneManager}}


The \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_scene_manager}{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Manager}} class provides many methods for developers getting the list of scenes, getting the list of conditions, getting the list of tasks, the list of cities, the list of scene log, etc.

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_scene_manager}{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Manager}} class provides many methods for developers getting the list of scenes, getting the list of conditions, getting the list of tasks, the list of cities, the list of scene log, etc. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_scene_core_kit_2_build_2_thing_smart_scene_core_kit_8xcframework_2ios-arm64__x86__644462cbe07e3f22d56e8ea3313339f51_source_l00040}{40}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_scene_core_kit_2_build_2_thing_smart_scene_core_kit_8xcframework_2ios-arm64__x86__644462cbe07e3f22d56e8ea3313339f51_source}{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Manager.\+h}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ (void) get\+Simple\+Scene\+List\+With\+Home\+Id\+: \begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(long long)}]{home\+Id }\item[{success\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{watchos-arm64__arm64__32__armv7k_2_thing_smart_scene_core_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_t_scene_defined_8h_a4caffb2983f7c6c8b4dc7e223bc2eb64}{Thing\+Scene\+Get\+List\+Completion}})}]{success }\item[{failure\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_af2b46bef0575729ec6391704cfc8a038}{Thing\+Failure\+Error}})}]{failure }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Get a simple list of scenes, including tap-\/to-\/run and automation. We can judge tap-\/to-\/run and automation scene by the entity\+Type of conditions property in \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_scene_model}{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Model}}, The scene is tap-\/to-\/run when the entity\+Type equal Auto\+Type\+Manual, otherwise it\textquotesingle{}s automation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The different between the simple scene list and scene list is less json data returned by the server.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em home\+Id} & The current home ID. \\
\hline
{\em success} & When successfully get the scene list, this block will be called and return \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_scene_model}{Thing\+Smart\+Scene\+Model}} list. \\
\hline
{\em failure} & When error occurred, this block will be called and return Thing\+Failure\+Error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
